###################################################
###################################################
###### Idea Variation 2 GA Idea Groups Admin
###################################################
###################################################

###################################################
###################################################
###### Ideagroup adm_1 Start
###################################################
###################################################

###############################################################
#### Select Idea Group adm_1
###############################################################


iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_1 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_1_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_1
###############################################################


iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_1 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_1_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_1 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}



iv2_ga_ideagroup_adm_1_1 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_1_1 }
				has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_1_1
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
			text = iv2_tt_no_points_for_idea_adm
			var:iv2_var_innovation_points_adm >= var:iv2_var_idea_cost_adm
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_country_modifier = { 
					modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_1_1 
					years = -1 
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
			text = iv2_tt_id_sub_points_adm
				change_variable = {
						name = iv2_var_innovation_points_adm
						subtract = iv2_idea_cost_adm
				}
			}
		}
	}
}


iv2_ga_ideagroup_adm_1_2 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_1_2 }
				has_country_modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_1_1
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
			text = iv2_tt_no_points_for_idea_adm
			var:iv2_var_innovation_points_adm >= var:iv2_var_idea_cost_adm
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_country_modifier = { 
					modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_1_2 
					years = -1 
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
			text = iv2_tt_id_sub_points_adm
				change_variable = {
						name = iv2_var_innovation_points_adm
						subtract = iv2_idea_cost_adm
				}
				trigger_event_non_silently = { id = IV2_calc.2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_country_modifier = { 
					modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_3_1 
					years = -1 
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
			text = iv2_tt_id_sub_points_adm
				change_variable = {
						name = iv2_var_innovation_points_adm
						subtract = iv2_idea_cost_adm
				}
			}
		}
	}

###############################################################
#### Select Idea Group adm_4
###############################################################


iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_4 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_4_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_4
###############################################################


iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_4 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_4_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_4 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_6 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_6_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_6
###############################################################


iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_6 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_6_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_6 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

###############################################################
#### Select Idea Group adm_8
###############################################################


iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_8 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
			government_type = government_type:republic
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_8_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_8
###############################################################


iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_8 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_8_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_8 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {			
					government_type = government_type:monarchy
					government_type = government_type:republic
					government_type = government_type:theocracy
					government_type = government_type:tribe
					government_type = government_type:steppe_horde
				}
			}	
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_9_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}

#### Select Idea Group adm_10

iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_10 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
			government_type = government_type:theocracy
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_10_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_10
###############################################################


iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_10 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_10_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_10 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_12 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
			NOT = {
				has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_13_1
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_12_1
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {

			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_17 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_17_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

###############################################################
#### Select Idea Group adm_19
###############################################################


iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_19 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_19_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_19
###############################################################


iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_19 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_19_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_19 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_21 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_21_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_21

iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_21 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_21_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_21 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

###############################################################
#### Select Idea Group adm_23
###############################################################


iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_23 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
			government_type = government_type:tribe
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_23_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_23
###############################################################


iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_23 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_23_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_23 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

		}
	}

		}

			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm

			}
		}
	}

	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

				has_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_29_1
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
			text = iv2_tt_no_points_for_idea_adm

			}

###############################################################
#### Select Idea Group adm_32
###############################################################


iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_32 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
			religion = religion:norse
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_32_1
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_32
###############################################################


iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_32 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_32_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_32 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

		}
	}

					modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_33_1 
					years = -1

				set_variable = {
					name = iv2_reli_ideagroup
					value = 1
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {

###############################################################
#### Select Idea Group adm_34
###############################################################


iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_34 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
			religion = religion:shinto
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_34_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_34
###############################################################


iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_34 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_34_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_34 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

###############################################################
#### Select Idea Group adm_36
###############################################################


iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_36 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
			OR = {
				religion = religion:nestorianism
				religion = religion:miaphysite
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_36_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_36
###############################################################


iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_36 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_36_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_36 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

###############################################################
#### Select Idea Group adm_38
###############################################################


iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_38 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
			OR = {
				religion = religion:sapmi_shamanism
				religion = religion:komi_paganism
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_38_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_38
###############################################################


iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_38 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_38_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_38 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

			}
			custom_tooltip = {

			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {

					modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_39_3

					name = iv2_reli_ideagroup
					value = 3
				}
			}

			text = iv2_tt_id_sub_points_adm
				change_variable = {
						name = iv2_var_innovation_points_adm
						subtract = iv2_idea_cost_adm
				}
				trigger_event_non_silently = { id = IV2_calc.2 }
			}
		}
	}

#### Select Idea Group adm_40
###############################################################


iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_40 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
			religion = religion:mari_paganism
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_40_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_40
###############################################################


iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_40 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_40_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_40 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_42 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
			religion = religion:manichaeism
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_42_1
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_42
###############################################################


iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_42 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_42_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_42 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

###############################################################
#### Select Idea Group adm_44
###############################################################


iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_44 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
			religion.group = religion_group:folk_african_group
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_44_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_44
###############################################################


iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_44 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_44_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_44 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_46 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
			religion = religion:anglican
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_46_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_46
###############################################################


iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_46 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_46_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_46 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_48 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
			religion.group = religion_group:folk_central_american_group
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_48_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_48
###############################################################


iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_48 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_48_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_48 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

#### Select Idea Group adm_50
###############################################################


iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_50 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
			religion.group = religion_group:folk_north_american_group
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_50_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###############################################################
#### De Select Idea Group adm_50
###############################################################


iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_50 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_50_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_50 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_52 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
			religion = religion:ibadi
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_52_1
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

#### De Select Idea Group adm_52

iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_52 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_52_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_52 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}

			}
			custom_tooltip = {
			text = iv2_tt_no_points_for_idea_adm
			var:iv2_var_innovation_points_adm >= var:iv2_var_idea_cost_adm
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_country_modifier = { 
					modifier = ideagroup_modifier_adm_53_7
					years = -1 
				}
				change_variable = {
					name = iv2_var_finished_idea_group_adm
					add = 1
				}	
				set_variable = {
					name = iv2_reli_ideagroup
					value = 7
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
			text = iv2_tt_id_sub_points_adm
				change_variable = {
						name = iv2_var_innovation_points_adm
						subtract = iv2_idea_cost_adm
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#### Select Idea Group adm_54

iv2_ga_select_ideagroup_adm_54 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = monthly
	ai_tick_frequency = 36

	automation_tick = monthly
	automation_tick_frequency = 1
	player_automated_category = governmentreform


	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		scope:actor = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = iv2_tt_no_available_idea_adm
				var:iv2_var_current_idea_group_adm > var:iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
			}
			religion.group = religion_group:folk_australian_group
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		add = {
			value = 1000
		}
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			set_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_54_1 
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

iv2_ga_deselect_ideagroup_adm_54 = {
	type = owncountry	

	ai_tick = never
	#ai_tick_frequency = 36

	potential = {
		
	}

	allow = {
		
	}
	
	effect = {
		scope:actor = {
			remove_variable = iv2_ideagroup_select_adm_54_1 
			iv2_scripted_effect_ig_revoke_adm_54 = yes
			change_variable = {
				name = iv2_var_current_picked_idea_group_adm
				subtract = 1
			}
		}	
	}
}
